<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To create a controlled Tabs component, manage the current selected tab using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> prop and update it when the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> event handler is called:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the tabs is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useTabs</code> hook. This way you can
access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="indicator" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Indicator</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To provide a visual cue for the selected tab, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tabs.Indicator</code> component:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="disabled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disabled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disabled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To disable a tab, simply pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> prop to the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tabs.Trigger</code> component:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="vertical" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#vertical"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Vertical</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The default orientation of the tabs is <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">horizontal</code>. To change the orientation, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation</code> prop to
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">vertical</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="lazy-mount" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#lazy-mount"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Lazy Mount</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Lazy mounting is a feature that allows the content of a tab to be rendered only when the tab is first activated. This is
useful for performance optimization, especially when tab content is large or complex. To enable lazy mounting, use the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> prop on the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Tabs.Content</code> component.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In addition, the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">unmountOnExit</code> prop can be used in conjunction with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> to unmount the tab content when the
tab is deactivated, freeing up resources. The next time the tab is activated, its content will be re-rendered.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="manual-activation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#manual-activation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Manual Activation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the tab can be selected when it receives focus from either the keyboard or pointer interaction. This is
called automatic tab activation.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In contrast, manual tab activation means the tab is selected with the</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><kbd>Enter</kbd> key or by clicking on the tab.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="links" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#links"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Links</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">asChild</code> prop to render tab triggers as anchor links. This is useful for SEO and allows tabs to work with
browser navigation.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a1hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="router-integration" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#router-integration"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Router Integration</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When using frameworks like Next.js, Remix, or React Router, controlling the active tabs based on the URL can be useful.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To achieve this, you need to do two things:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> prop to the current URL path.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Listen to the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> event and update the URL path.</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s an example using Remix Router</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { Tabs } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/&lt;framework&gt;/tabs&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { useLocation, useNavigate, Link } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@remix-run/react&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">export</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> default</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> function</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> App</span><span style="color:#FFA657">() </span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">pathname</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useLocation</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> navigate</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useNavigate</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> lastPathFragment</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> pathname.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">substring</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(pathname.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">lastIndexOf</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;/&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">+</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> 1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> activeTab</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> lastPathFragment.</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">length</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> &gt;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> 0</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> ?</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> lastPathFragment </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">:</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;homepage&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Root</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">      value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">activeTab</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">      onValueChange</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({ </span><span style="color:#FFA657">value</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> }) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">        navigate</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">`/${</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> ===</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;home&#x27;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> ?</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;&#x27;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> :</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> value</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">}`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      }</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.List</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> asChild</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;home&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> to</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Home&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> asChild</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;page-1&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> to</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;page-1&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Page 1&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> asChild</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;page-2&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> to</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;page-2&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Page 2&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Link</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.List</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Tabs.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Prop</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Default</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">activationMode</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;automatic&#x27;</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;manual&#x27; | &#x27;automatic&#x27;</code><p class="text">The activation mode of the tabs. <h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/tabs/" class="link">Tabs WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Key</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Tab</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">When focus moves onto the tabs, focuses the active trigger. When a trigger is focused, moves focus to the active content.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowDown</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the next trigger in vertical orientation and activates its associated content.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowRight</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the next trigger in horizontal orientation and activates its associated content.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowUp</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the previous trigger in vertical orientation and activates its associated content.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowLeft</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the previous trigger in horizontal orientation and activates its associated content.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Home</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves the\n`onValueChange` event handler is called:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = useState\u003cstring | null\u003e('account')\n  return (\n    \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} value={value} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n          Account\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n          Password\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n          Billing\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Make changes to your account here.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Change your password here.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Manage your billing and payment details.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/solid/tabs'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal\u003cstring | null\u003e('account')\n  return (\n    \u003cTabs.Root class={styles.Root} value={value()} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n          Account\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n          Password\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n          Billing\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Make changes to your account here.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Change your password here.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Manage your billing and payment details.\n      \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tabs } from class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the tabs is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useTabs` hook. This way you can\naccess the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs, useTabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const tabs = useTabs({ defaultValue: 'account' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eselected: {tabs.value}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={tabs}\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n          \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n            Account\n          \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n            Password\n          \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n            Billing\n          \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n          Make changes to your account here.\n        \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n          Change your password here.\n        \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n          Manage your billing and payment details.\n        \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Tabs.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs, useTabs } from '@ark-ui/solid/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Disabled\n\nTo disable a tab, simply pass the `disabled` prop to the `Tabs.Trigger` component:\n\n**Example: disabled-tab**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const DisabledTab = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\" disabled\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/solid/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const DisabledTab = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\" disabled\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger   Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/vue/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List :class=\"styles.List\"\u003e\n disabled\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tabs'\n \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\" disabled\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Vertical\n\nThe default orientation of the tabs is `horizontal`. To change the orientation, set the `orientation` prop to\n`vertical`.\n\n**Example: vertical**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} orientation=\"vertical\" defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n value=\"account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" value=\"password\"\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tabs'\n  import styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cTabs.Root account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Lazy Mount\n\nLazy mounting is a feature that allows the content of a tab to be rendered only when the tab is first activated. This is\nuseful for performance optimization, especially when tab content is large or complex. To enable lazy mounting, use the\n`lazyMount` prop on the `Tabs.Content` component.\n\nIn addition, the `unmountOnExit` prop can be used in conjunction with `lazyMount` to unmount the tab content when the\ntab is deactivated, freeing up resources. The next time the tab is activated, its content will be re-rendered.\n\n**Example: lazy-mount**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} lazyMount unmountOnExit defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Indicator className={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/solid/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root class={styles.Root} lazyMount unmountOnExit defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/vue/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" lazy-mount unmount-on-exit default-value=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List :class=\"styles.List\"\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.TriggerIndicator\" value=\"account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.TriggerIndicator\" value=\"password\"\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.TriggerIndicator\" value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tabs'\n  import styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cTabs.Root class={styles.Root} lazyMount unmountOnExit defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"password\"\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.TriggerIndicator} value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Indicator class={styles.Indicator} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Manual Activation\n\nBy default, the tab can be selected when it receives focus from either the keyboard or pointer interaction. This is\ncalled automatic tab activation.\n\nIn contrast, manual tab activation means the tab is selected with the\n\n\u003ckbd\u003eEnter\u003c/kbd\u003e key or by clicking on the tab.\n\n**Example: manual-activation**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const ManualActivation = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} activationMode=\"manual\" defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content className={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/solid/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const ManualActivation = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root class={styles.Root} activationMode=\"manual\" defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\"\u003e\n        Account\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"password\"\u003e\n        Password\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger class={styles.Trigger} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n        Billing\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"account\"\u003e\n      Make changes to your account here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003e\n      Change your password here.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003e\n      Manage your billing and payment details.\n    \u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/vue/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" activation-mode=\"manual\" default-value=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List :class=\"styles.List\"\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" value=\"account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" value=\"password\"\u003ePassword\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\" value=\"billing\"\u003eBilling\u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"account\"\u003eMake changes to your account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.Content :class=\"styles.Content\" value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/svelte/tabs'\n  import styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cTabs.Root account here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"password\"\u003eChange your password here.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n  \u003cTabs.Content class={styles.Content} value=\"billing\"\u003eManage your billing and payment details.\u003c/Tabs.Content\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Links\n\nUse the `asChild` prop to render tab triggers as anchor links. This is useful for SEO and allows tabs to work with\nbrowser navigation.\n\n**Example: links**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/react/tabs'\nimport styles from 'styles/tabs.module.css'\n\nexport const Links = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cTabs.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"account\"\u003e\n    \u003cTabs.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger className={styles.Trigger} value=\"account\" asChild\u003e\n        \u003ca href=\"#account\"\u003eAccount\u003c/a\u003e\n      \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cTabs.Trigger on the URL can be useful.\n\nTo achieve this, you need to do two things:\n\n- Set the `value` prop to the current URL path.\n- Listen to the `onValueChange` event and update the URL path.\n\nHere's an example using Remix Router\n\n```tsx\nimport { Tabs } from '@ark-ui/\u003cframework\u003e/tabs'\nimport { useLocation, useNavigate, Link } from '@remix-run/react'\n\nexport default function App() {\n  const { pathname } = useLocation()\n  const navigate = useNavigate()\n  const lastPathFragment = pathname.substring(pathname.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)\n  const activeTab = lastPathFragment.length \u003e 0 ? lastPathFragment : 'homepage'\n\n  return (\n    \u003cTabs.Root\n      value={activeTab}\n      onValueChange={({ value }) =\u003e {\n        navigate(`/${value === 'home' ? '' : value}`)\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cTabs.List\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger asChild value=\"home\"\u003e\n          \u003cLink to=\"\"\u003eHome\u003c/Link\u003e\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger asChild value=\"page-1\"\u003e\n          \u003cLink to=\"page-1\"\u003ePage 1\u003c/Link\u003e\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cTabs.Trigger asChild value=\"page-2\"\u003e\n          \u003cLink to=\"page-2\"\u003ePage 2\u003c/Link\u003e\n        \u003c/Tabs.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003c/Tabs.List\u003e\n    \u003c/Tabs.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `activationMode` | `'manual' | 'automatic'` | No | The activation mode of the tabs. Can be `manual` or `automatic`\n- `manual`: Tabs are activated when clicked or press `enter` key.\n- `automatic`: Tabs are activated when receiving focus |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `composite` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tab is composite |\n| `defaultValue` | `string` | No | The initial selected tab value when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the selected tab value. |\n| `deselectable` | `boolean` | No | Whether the active tab can be deselected when clicking on it. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  trigger: (value: string) =\u003e string\n  list: string\n  content: (value: string) =\u003e string\n  indicator: string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the tabs. Useful for composition. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `loopFocus` | `boolean` | No | Whether the keyboard navigation will loop from last tab to first, and vice versa. |\n| `navigate` | `(details: NavigateDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function to navigate to the selected tab when clicking on it.\nUseful if tab triggers are anchor elements. |\n| `onFocusChange` | `(details: FocusChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback to be called when the focused tab changes |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback to be called when the selected/active tab changes |\n| `orientation` | `'horizontal' | 'vertical'` | No | The orientation of the tabs. Can be `horizontal` or `vertical`\n- `horizontal`: only left and right arrow key navigation will work.\n- `vertical`: only up and down arrow key navigation will work. |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n| `value` | `string` | No | The controlled selected tab value |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | tabs |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `string` | The value of the tab that is currently focused. |\n| `setValue` | `(value: string) =\u003e void` | Sets the value of the tabs. |\n| `clearValue` | `VoidFunction` | Clears the value of the tabs. |\n| `setIndicatorRect` | `(value: string) =\u003e void` | Sets the indicator rect to the tab with the given value |\n| `syncTabIndex` | `VoidFunction` | Synchronizes the tab index of the content element.\nUseful when rendering tabs within a select or combobox |\n| `focus` | `VoidFunction` | Set focus on the selected tab trigger |\n| `selectNext` | `(fromValue?: string) =\u003e void` | Selects the next tab |\n| `selectPrev` | `(fromValue?: string) =\u003e void` | Selects the previous tab |\n| `getTriggerState` | `(props: TriggerProps) =\u003e TriggerState` | Returns the state of the trigger with the given props |\n\n\n## Accessibility\n\nComplies with the [Tabs WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/tabs/).\n\n### Keyboard
